<span id="freeTextContainer9127653172303755863"><b>Reread 4-6-17</b><br/><br/>Had a friend sit me down and look at this from a different perspective. So I did. Turned out to like it somewhat. I still can't look past somethings but I will move on to the next book. <br/><br/>~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~<br/><b>Original Review</b><br/>My edition: Kindle<br/>Pages: 268<br/>Series: Seraph Black #1<br/>Rating: No rating<br/><br/>Review: I had to take a little break from the Derek and Sofia drama so I thought this might work. Well I chose this book because it was recommended to me since I liked C.L. Stone Academy serie</span>
  <span id="freeText9127653172303755863" style="display:none"><b>Reread 4-6-17</b><br /><br />Had a friend sit me down and look at this from a different perspective. So I did. Turned out to like it somewhat. I still can't look past somethings but I will move on to the next book. <br /><br />~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~<br /><b>Original Review</b><br />My edition: Kindle<br />Pages: 268<br />Series: Seraph Black #1<br />Rating: No rating<br /><br />Review: I had to take a little break from the Derek and Sofia drama so I thought this might work. Well I chose this book because it was recommended to me since I liked C.L. Stone Academy series, both Ghost Bird and Scarab Beetle. Well come to find out that these two book series have way to much in common.<br /><br />t seemed like both series of the Academy were put together in one book and a fantasy atmosphere was thrown in. Most of the reviews I've seen that saw the say saw more of the Ghost Bird but I see more of The Scarab Beetle in this. I didn't see if this was a retelling or not but the similarities are to much to be coincidence.<br /><br />Ex: Corey and Brandon (Scarab Beetle) are identical twins that are hard to tell apart but Kayli can by looking at their eyes. Brandon's seems to have more sad eyes than Corey.<br />Miro and Silas are identical twins that Seph can tell apart by their eyes. Silas has more sad and pain eyes than Miro<br /><br />Ex: Sang (Ghost Bird) can tell her boys are near hear by their scents with out having to look up.<br />Seph can tell when Miro or Noah are near by their scent.<br /><br />Ex: Kayli (Scarab Beetle) lives with her brother and alcoholic father. Everything went down hill after her mother died. She has to work different jobs so they have food and pay bills.<br />Seph lives with her brother and alcoholic father. Everything went bad when her mother died. She has to work at a club so they have food.<br /><br />That isn't all the similarities. It is just a few that I can think of on the spot.<br /><br /> I don't mean to insult anyone but that is what I got out of this. I just felt that this was a little to close to the Academy series to my comfort. I have decided not to rate it. I don't know if I will continue on with this series. I'm going to sit and maul on it for a little while.</span>

        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1484114147?book_show_action=true">Dec 28, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mita" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mita" href="/user/show/17953641-mita">Mita</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer14572018011756456349">This is a bizarre one. <br/><br/>The premise is intriguing; a girl, Seraph, brought up in a harsh life, made tough to survive, all the while carrying a secret so bizarre there is no one safe to tell, finds herself caught between not TWO, but FOUR individuals who bolster her self-confidence and makes her feel safe despite her harsh life and yet, when a stalker is introduced to said life, she can't tell who threaten her survival more, the guys or her stalker.<br/>very cool.<br/><br/>BUT, there is a confusion that comes wi</span>
  <span id="freeText14572018011756456349" style="display:none">This is a bizarre one. <br /><br />The premise is intriguing; a girl, Seraph, brought up in a harsh life, made tough to survive, all the while carrying a secret so bizarre there is no one safe to tell, finds herself caught between not TWO, but FOUR individuals who bolster her self-confidence and makes her feel safe despite her harsh life and yet, when a stalker is introduced to said life, she can't tell who threaten her survival more, the guys or her stalker.<br />very cool.<br /><br />BUT, there is a confusion that comes with reading this book. In part, the confusion lends itself to further connecting with Seraph's character and her current predicament, but, there are certain parts that seem too confusing and possibly the product of poor writing. I'm hoping for the former to be mostly true, in any case.<br /><br />DESPITE that little bit of WTHeck, this is a very good story. The characters are strange but likable. Seraph is good combination of tough and vulnerable--no wussy, whimpy, straight up annoying you-just-want-to-bash-her-head-in kind of main girl char--and I did mention FOUR dudes, hot in their own rights... right?<br /><br />all together, Charcoal Tears is a worthy read and a definite Recommend from ME!!<br /><br />(sorry for the wait on my review--holidays :p lol)</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer14831032921500237735">What to say...what to say...this is one of those books that keeps you hooked till the end. Yes, it's annoying to not grasp what is exactly going on and yes it was annoying that the lead chick didn't ask the questions and demand the answers like I thought she should but it is what kept me reading kind of. <br/><br/>I will admit I still don't get the whole bond thing...the whole 4 guys thing kind of weirds me out a little.   <span id="freeText14831032921500237735" style="display:none">What to say...what to say...this is one of those books that keeps you hooked till the end. Yes, it's annoying to not grasp what is exactly going on and yes it was annoying that the lead chick didn't ask the questions and demand the answers like I thought she should but it is what kept me reading kind of. <br /><br />I will admit I still don't get the whole bond thing...the whole 4 guys thing kind of weirds me out a little. I actually thought there would be a twist at some point and Silas would be the one and only considering the way they seemed to feel. It was kind of unnerving to read that Miro was so heartbroken kissing her and all. Oh, then she wasn't suppose to tell Tabby what she is but she did and Miro and Silas didn't even acknowledge that she told Tabby which was odd. I dunno. I will definitely read the next book. I loved all the characters and it's just an interesting concept. I actually dreamt about this book and had to go back this morning and re-read some items lol. <br /><br />I was real bummed to know the second book wasn't out yet!! </span>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:

<span id="freeTextContainer2758529366436263041"><b> 2.5 stars</b><br/><br/>So I read this because this author had a hand in writing trickery and I thought this would be awesome.Well, sometimes co-writing a book really does work. I liked this but not as much as I did Trickery. <br/><br/>The entire book and I still don't know what is going on, who's bad or good. What the bond thing is all about. I don't even think I like the MMC or the FC, they were just too bland for me. I also did not like the way Seraph never questioned anything, they tell her to leave her family , sh</span>
  <span id="freeText2758529366436263041" style="display:none"><b> 2.5 stars</b><br /><br />So I read this because this author had a hand in writing trickery and I thought this would be awesome.Well, sometimes co-writing a book really does work. I liked this but not as much as I did Trickery. <br /><br />The entire book and I still don't know what is going on, who's bad or good. What the bond thing is all about. I don't even think I like the MMC or the FC, they were just too bland for me. I also did not like the way Seraph never questioned anything, they tell her to leave her family , she agrees. She sees tons of pictures of her, taken without her permission but she only has a tiny freak out session and then goes back to normal, 4 guys seem to have stalked her for months but she doesn't care because she feels it's "meant" to be. Ehh<br /><br />I'll read the next one,hopefully it gets better.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer17832452795578133838"><strong>Love the idea</strong><br/><br/>I am all for the reverse harem story Line - however, this was extremely frustrating to read. You Will not get one. Single. Answer. NOT ONE. And on top of that you get a huge cliffhanger. Christ. Some times I wonder if authors Think the only Way to get the readers to buy the next book is to make sure the first one ends with a cliffhanger and a billion questions. What happened to wanting to buy the next in the series because the first one was awesome?<br/><br/>Also, it is very juvenile - ridicu</span>
  <span id="freeText17832452795578133838" style="display:none"><strong>Love the idea</strong><br /><br />I am all for the reverse harem story Line - however, this was extremely frustrating to read. You Will not get one. Single. Answer. NOT ONE. And on top of that you get a huge cliffhanger. Christ. Some times I wonder if authors Think the only Way to get the readers to buy the next book is to make sure the first one ends with a cliffhanger and a billion questions. What happened to wanting to buy the next in the series because the first one was awesome?<br /><br />Also, it is very juvenile - ridiculously so considering Two of the guys are 25. I would have loved for it to be more na in-sted of ya.<br /><br />Lastly, it Will remind you a great deal of "The academy" by CS Stone. A great deal.</span>

<div class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground">Readers also enjoyed</h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent"><div class='bookCarousel'>
<div class='carouselRow' style='width: 3600px'>
<ul>
<li class='cover' id='bookCover_35721433'>
<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/35721433-the-vixen-s-lead"><img alt="The Vixen&#39;s Lead (Kit Davenport, #1)" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/books/1500672341l/35721433._SX98_.jpg" />
</a>

  
<script type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8">
//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('Ja3hJMCa5d0ns+NQ6VujoJvv/iJ3V7feA2Sn7qpVskjbN5QIYyXYEtkTZWwsQ8ebtTLSoEy6c1mm4HpMhhYpqw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {

  }

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer8017426987340816542">Jane is a caffeine-addicted manic stuffed into the body of a passably-functioning human being. She also happens to be a Wall Street Journal bestselling author, and has sold over a million ebooks worldwide. Living in Australia with a few cacti and a miniature dachshund [see: dictator], she spends her time writing books … and then telling everyone not to read them. </span>
